LAW DEPARTMENT
LIST OF NOTARIES APPOINTED AND IN PRACTICE AT THE BEGINNING OF THE YEAR 2011
(See rule 17)
[G.O. Ms. No. 48, Law (Administration) Department, 28th January 2011.]
No. II(2)/LAW/44 (b)/2011.
In exercise of  the powers conferred by section 6 of the Notaries Act, 1952 (Central Act LIII of 1952),
the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby publishes the following list of notaries appointed by the Government of
Tamil Nadu and in practice at the beginning of the year 2011 :—
